# Push candidate validation: continuous-rally stability + timing-window robustness

> Research tool output (return-studio.html), not game4.html acceptance. Does not modify return-studio.html.
Updated: 2026-07-13T10:25:29.871Z
Presets: 11 (11-preset calibration set, same exclusions as push-tilty-sweep-calibration.js: no_spin_long_forehand, no_spin_long_backhand, backspin_short_forehand_2, backspin_short_backhand_2, backspin_short_backhand)
Param sets compared: Deployed baseline (tiltY=0.8, driveScale=1.0) | Candidate (tiltY=1.0, driveScale=0.8) | Candidate (tiltY=1.1, driveScale=0.8)

## Layer 1: Continuous-rally stability (runRallyReal, maxRounds=60)

Per param set, per preset: rounds survived before failure, first-round vs max outgoing speed/apex (growth ratio = max/first; ~1.0 = stable, >>1 = diverging).

## Layer 2: Timing-window robustness

Per param set, per preset: size of the valid post-bounce hit window (points[i].y > TABLE.top, between receiver bounce and next bounce/end), pass-rate across that whole window, and whether the one canonical findPushHitIndex point itself passes.

### Deployed baseline (tiltY=0.8, driveScale=1.0)

preset | window size | canonical idx in window | canonical passes | window pass-rate (ok/total)
--- | --- | --- | --- | ---
backspin_long_backhand | 55 | true | true | 100% (55/55)
sidebackspin_long_forehand | 39 | true | true | 100% (39/39)
sidebackspin_half_long_forehand | 40 | true | true | 100% (40/40)
sidebackspin_half_long_backhand | 39 | true | true | 100% (39/39)
sidebackspin_long_backhand | 38 | true | true | 100% (38/38)
sidebackspin_long_forehand_2 | 40 | true | true | 100% (40/40)
sidebackspin_long_forehand_3 | 40 | true | true | 100% (40/40)
backspin_long_forehand | 42 | true | true | 100% (42/42)
backspin_long_forehand_2 | 50 | true | true | 98% (49/50)
backspin_short_forehand | 50 | true | true | 80% (40/50)
sidebackspin_short_forehand | 49 | true | true | 83.7% (41/49)

Aggregate window pass-rate: 96.1% (463/482 samples across all presets). Canonical-point pass count: 11/11 presets.
